#####1#####
Based on the provided CVE description, let's analyze the base metrics for the CVSS v3.1 Base Score:

- **Attack Vector (AV)**: The attack vector is Local (L) since the vulnerability is exploited by an attacker who must be able to interact with the affected system.
- **Attack Complexity (AC)**: The attack complexity is Low (L) as exploiting the vulnerability does not require specialized conditions.
- **Privileges Required (PR)**: Privileges Required is None (N) as the attacker can exploit the vulnerability without any special access.
- **User Interaction (UI)**: User Interaction is not required (N) for the exploit to be successful.
- **Scope (S)**: The scope is Unchanged (U) as the impact is limited to the original impacted component.
- **Confidentiality (C)**: The impact on Confidentiality is None (N) as there is no impact on confidentiality.
- **Integrity (I)**: The impact on Integrity is High (H) as the vulnerability can lead to a complete compromise of the system.
- **Availability (A)**: The impact on Availability is High (H) as the vulnerability can lead to a denial of service.

Therefore, the final CVSS v3.1 vector string for this CVE is:
CVSS:3.1/AV:L/AC:L/PR:N/UI:N/S:U/C:N/I:H/A:H

#####5#####
Based on the provided CVE description, let's analyze the CVSS v3.1 Base Score metrics:

- **Attack Vector (AV)**: Network (N) - The attack is network-based.
- **Attack Complexity (AC)**: Low (L) - The attack complexity is low as it can be exploited by authenticated attackers with contributor-level and above permissions.
- **Privileges Required (PR)**: Low (L) - The attacker requires low privileges to exploit the vulnerability.
- **User Interaction (UI)**: None (N) - No user interaction is required for the attack.
- **Scope (S)**: Unchanged (U) - The scope remains unchanged after the attack.
- **Confidentiality (C)**: Low (L) - The impact on confidentiality is low as it allows for arbitrary web scripts injection.
- **Integrity (I)**: High (H) - The impact on integrity is high as arbitrary web scripts can be injected and executed.
- **Availability (A)**: None (N) - The impact on availability is none.

Calculating the CVSS v3.1 Base Score:
- Base Score = 3.1*(AV + AC + PR + UI + S + C + I + A)
- Base Score = 3.1*(0.4 + 0.22 + 0.22 + 0 + 0 + 0.22 + 0.66 + 0)
- Base Score = 3.1*1.72
- Base Score = 5.332

Therefore, the final CVSS v3.1 vector string for this vulnerability is:
CVSS:3.1/AV:N/AC:L/PR:L/UI:N/S:U/C:L/I:H/A:N

- Privileges Required (PR): Privileges Required is Low (L) as the attacker does not need any special privileges to exploit the vulnerability.

- Scope (S): The scope is Unchanged (U) as the impact is limited to the container and does not affect the host system.

- Integrity (I): Integrity impact is Low (L) as the attacker could potentially modify files within the container.
- Availability (A): Availability impact is None (N) as there is no impact on availability.

- **Confidentiality (C)**: The impact on Confidentiality is None (N) as there is no unauthorized disclosure of information.
- **Integrity (I)**: The impact on Integrity is Low (L) as the vulnerability could potentially cause data corruption.
- **Availability (A)**: The impact on Availability is None (N) as there is no impact on the availability of resources.

Calculating the CVSS v3.1 Base Score:
- Base Score = 3.1 * [(0.35 * AV) + (0.35 * AC) + (0.3 * PR) + (0.3 * UI) + (S)]
- Base Score = 3.1 * [(0.35 * 0.4) + (0.35 * 0.3) + (0.3 * 0) + (0.3 * 0) + 0]
- Base Score = 3.1 * [0.14 + 0.105 + 0 + 0]
- Base Score = 3.1 * 0.245
- Base Score = 0.7595

Therefore, the CVSS v3.1 vector string for this vulnerability is: CVSS:3.1/AV:L/AC:L/PR:N/UI:N/S:U/C:N/I:L/A:N

- Confidentiality (C): High (H)
- Integrity (I): High (H)
- Availability (A): High (H)

CVSS v3.1 Base Score Calculation:
- Base Score = 8.0
- Impact Subscore = 1 - [(1 - 0.6) * (1 - 0.6) * (1 - 0.6)] = 0.936
- Exploitability Subscore = 8.22 * 0.56 = 4.5912
- Base Score = Roundup(Minimum[(Impact + Exploitability), 10]) = Roundup(Minimum[(0.936 + 4.5912), 10]) = Roundup(5.5272) = 6.0

Summarized Metric Values:
- AV: N
- AC: H
- PR: H
- UI: N
- S: C
- C: H
- I: H
- A: H

Final CVSS v3.1 Vector String:
CVSS:3.1/AV:N/AC:H/PR:H/UI:N/S:C/C:H/I:H/A:H

- **Integrity (I)**: The impact on integrity is usually Low (L) for XSS vulnerabilities as they can manipulate the content of a web page but may not directly modify data on the server.
- **Availability (A)**: The impact on availability is typically None (N) for XSS vulnerabilities as they do not directly impact the availability of the system.

- **Attack Vector (AV)**: The attack vector is adjacent (A) since the attacker needs to be able to trick a site administrator into performing an action.
- **Attack Complexity (AC)**: The attack complexity is low (L) as the attacker only needs to trick the site administrator into clicking on a link.
- **Privileges Required (PR)**: Privileges required are low (L) as the attacker does not need any special privileges.
- **User Interaction (UI)**: User interaction is required (R) as the attacker needs to trick the site administrator into clicking on a link.
- **Scope (S)**: The scope is unchanged (U) as the vulnerability does not impact resources outside the immediate security scope.
- **Confidentiality (C)**: The impact on confidentiality is low (L) as the vulnerability does not directly lead to the exposure of sensitive information.
- **Integrity (I)**: The impact on integrity is high (H) as the attacker can deactivate the plugin's stripe integration settings.
- **Availability (A)**: The impact on availability is none (N) as the vulnerability does not directly impact the availability of resources.

Calculating the CVSS v3.1 Base Score:

- Impact = 6.1 (High Integrity) + 0 (Low Confidentiality) + 0 (None Availability) = 6.1
- Exploitability = 2.8 (Low Attack Complexity) + 0 (Low Privileges Required) + 0 (User Interaction Required) = 2.8
- Base Score = 3.1 * [(0.85 * 6.1 + 0.15 * 2.8) - 1.43] = 7.15

- **Availability (A)**: The availability impact is "None (N)" as the vulnerability does not impact the availability of the system.
